CREATE TABLE sustainability_metrics (id INT PRIMARY KEY, metric_name TEXT, description TEXT, target_value FLOAT, actual_value FLOAT)

CREATE TABLE environmental_impact (id INT PRIMARY KEY, name TEXT, description TEXT, impact_type TEXT)

CREATE TABLE sustainability_goals (id INT PRIMARY KEY, goal_name TEXT, target TEXT, completion_date DATE)</t><s>ALTER TABLE sustainability_goals RENAME TO goals_table</s>
